The converted document will be received by the mobile app and displayed within an app viewer, which will not allow to print or forward the protected document.\r\n\r\nDocuments can be stored on the device with strong encryption, in order to be viewed later even when offline.\r\n\r\n\r\nREQUIREMENTS:\r\n* glueckkanja.com RMS Rendering Server deployed in the corporate network\r\n* Microsoft Active
